| 2:07:52| and we've concluded that the county may constitutionally regulate electronic billboards.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090323part2?start=7672)|

| 2:09:28| the static hold time for each image on the sign,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090323part2?start=7768)|
